-------------------------------------

Build: #2715

Duration: 23 minutes and 59 seconds
Commit: 65be5fe (ocaml-mccs)
Author: Louis Gesbert
Message: Fix 'make lib-ext', remove no longer needed dependencies, add ocaml-mccs

- camlp4 shouldn't be needed (was only a stale dependencies of older
  cudf releases)
- Thanks to @dbuenzli, we don't require jsonm/uchar/uutf anymore
- Switch to newer (dev) cmdliner enables build without topkg (and avoids
  the dependency cycle)

NB: Due to mccs, you may no longer build without a C++ compiler and glpk
installed. It will be made optional.

NB2: the bootstrap might still be broken
